  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2068129303" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2068129303" />
    <a title="Whispering Stories" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20354973-whispering-stories"><img alt="Whispering Stories" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548065529p2/20354973.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2068129303?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whispering Stories" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whispering Stories" href="/user/show/20354973-whispering-stories">Whispering Stories</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2068129303" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6299817000030243566">Blair Walker is having one hell of a day, she has just been gazumped for the job she has been working hard towards for years, by someone who bought their way to the top. She is then fired from the job she was currently doing, and then her boyfriend of three years, takes her to dinner, and dumps her for another woman.<br/><br/>Down on her look she takes to the local bar, where after reading a list of 15 items she was told never to do, she decides it’s time to cross them off one by one, starting with ‘Never</span>
  <span id="freeText6299817000030243566" style="display:none">Blair Walker is having one hell of a day, she has just been gazumped for the job she has been working hard towards for years, by someone who bought their way to the top. She is then fired from the job she was currently doing, and then her boyfriend of three years, takes her to dinner, and dumps her for another woman.<br /><br />Down on her look she takes to the local bar, where after reading a list of 15 items she was told never to do, she decides it’s time to cross them off one by one, starting with ‘Never get Drunk’. Trouble is she wakes up in a stranger’s apartment, a man who promises that they didn’t sleep together, but does offer her a job.<br /><br />With no money to cover her half of the rent for the flat she shares with her best friend Nikki, she agrees to the job of ‘Beauty and Fashion editor’ of an online magazine. The only problem is, her boss is quite hunky. Can she keep her hands to herself, and also get through the lists of things that she should never do?<br /><br />I have read a few Camilla Isley novels, all have been imaginative, exciting and laugh out loud, this one is just the same.<br /><br />Blair is extremely likeable. She thinks that it is time to let her hair down and stop being so mature about everything. When she didn’t get the editorial job that she had been working towards for years, something in her just clicked, enough was enough. She has tried to live by a set of rules, but they have gotten her nowhere. Now it was time to break them.<br /><br />Richard runs the online magazine. He is tall, handsome and rubs shoulders with celebrities. He is smitten with Blair, but after a past love affair went sour, he doesn’t date, just more of a one night stand sort of guy. At least he can’t get hurt that way, or so he thinks.<br /><br />This book is pure chick-lit from beginning to end. I loved everything about it, from the perfect New York scenery, to the amazing characters that have a lot of depth to them. The writing is faultless and the plot, including the subplots, are most certainly intriguing.<br /><br />Each chapter is dedicated to an item on Blair’s List. Each new chapter had me eager to discover just what she would do to cross that item off. Plus for those romantics out there, the will they, won’t they, love action is ever present for you to enjoy.<br /><br />A light-hearted book that will hold you captive to the pages, and won’t let you go until the very last word.<br /><br />Reviewed by Stacey on <a href="http://www.whisperingstories.com" rel="nofollow noopener">www.whisperingstories.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6299817000030243566" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2725280589" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4771388911636492940"><b>4 <i>totally had me chuckling</i> stars</b><br/><br/><b>Read my entire review here on my blog <a href='https://readingunderstreetlamps.wordpress.com/2019/02/22/i-have-never-camilla-isley/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Readin' Under Street-Lamps</a>.</b><br/><br/>Blair Walker’s carefully planned out life burns down to the ground when she loses her job, and her boyfriend of three years leaves her for his secretary, all on the same day. *cue eyeroll* Deciding to throw all her rules in the air, and finally enjoying life, her new plan of action is doing exactly opposite of what her list states.<br/><br/>And thus begins a really hilarious and heart-warming tale of a woman f</span>
  <span id="freeText4771388911636492940" style="display:none"><b>4 <i>totally had me chuckling</i> stars</b><br /><br /><b>Read my entire review here on my blog <a href="https://readingunderstreetlamps.wordpress.com/2019/02/22/i-have-never-camilla-isley/" rel="nofollow noopener">Readin' Under Street-Lamps</a>.</b><br /><br />Blair Walker’s carefully planned out life burns down to the ground when she loses her job, and her boyfriend of three years leaves her for his secretary, all on the same day. *cue eyeroll* Deciding to throw all her rules in the air, and finally enjoying life, her new plan of action is doing exactly opposite of what her list states.<br /><br />And thus begins a really hilarious and heart-warming tale of a woman finding herself, adopting a puppy who understands english, and falling in love with the most unavailable man- her boss.<br /><br />Because of course.<br /><br />And like I said, the cliches are a bit obvious, but all the characters- and I’m not just talking about Blair and Richard (the boss) and Chevron (the pup), but even the side characters were just so much full of personality, that it was impossible to not be utterly charmed by this story.<br /><br />And on top of that Blair was just such a likable character. Yeah she has to start her life from scratch at 29, but she never moans and groans and bitches about it. She just takes it as it is and sasses right through it. When she falls in love with Richard, who is a serious commitment-phobe, she doesn’t let it deter her, and she says it best— “I don’t quit. I don’t run away from the things that scare me. I run after what I want.”<br /><br />In a nutshell, I could totally see myself as Blair. That is how relatable she was written. And for that I have to totally give it to Isley.<br /><br />I have never read Camilla Isley’s works before, for obvious reasons. And I am very very happy that I actually found her, even if it was just due to my bored shenanigans on NetGalley— you know what I mean *wink wink*<br /><br />I Have Never delivers exactly what it promises- a loud laughter with almost every chapter, and heart. It gives you so so much of heart that you can’t help but just feel good by the end. This is a book that is going to make you take your own “NO-NO List” and mutiny against it.<br /><br /><b>ARC provided by the author via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</b></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2035399372" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2035399372?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Gilbey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Gilbey" href="/user/show/5801320-rachel-gilbey">Rachel Gilbey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2035399372" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10719999198460320907">My smile didn't leave my face for the entirety of I Have Never, which is essentially Blair Walker attempting to do the opposite of all the rules she has lived behind for her life. However after one disastrous day where Blair loses both boyfriend and job, she starts to think she may need to change her life philosophies. <br/><br/>What follows is hilarious, especially the scene when she wakes up the next morning after her awful day. Every chapter is subtitles with a different item from Blair's list which is</span>
  <span id="freeText10719999198460320907" style="display:none">My smile didn't leave my face for the entirety of I Have Never, which is essentially Blair Walker attempting to do the opposite of all the rules she has lived behind for her life. However after one disastrous day where Blair loses both boyfriend and job, she starts to think she may need to change her life philosophies. <br /><br />What follows is hilarious, especially the scene when she wakes up the next morning after her awful day. Every chapter is subtitles with a different item from Blair's list which is the item being illustrated or directly opposed in that chapter. <br /><br />In amongst the book you will encounter an incredibly intelligent dog, that seems to understand human english far too well. There is an epic break up scene, a scene full of sexual tension, a plot line that shows how savvy Blair can be when she puts her mind to it, plus a whole lot more. <br /><br />This may be the second book in the First Comes Love series, but it can easily be read as a standalone. I can safely say this as I didn't even realise how this was connected to the first book (which I read around its release), to this one, until I read the note from the author at the end of the book! <br /><br />This is a sparkling, fun, quick and easy to read story that I enjoyed every moment of. <br /><br />Thank you so much to Camilla Isley for this copy which I have reviewed honestly and voluntarily.</span>

<div id="review_2533115411" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2533115411" />
    <a title="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere"><img alt="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600017870p2/4386752.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2533115411?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" href="/user/show/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere">Ezinwanyi Chinyere</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/40773551-i-have-never">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=review-books-completed">review-books-completed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=giveaways">giveaways</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2533115411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7337700077405699607">Review posted at <a href='https://wp.me/p9u34A-5e' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Chaise and Lounge Blog</a><br/><br/>This audiobook was easy to follow and was a fun listen until I got the end. It was a happy ending but it reinforced that office romances can never remain secret and can make the workplace tense when there is a disharmony.<br/><br/>Blair Walker was a girl who followed all of society rules of how a refined lady should behave. Living by that good girl code led her to losing her dreams to another who was willing to use all in her arsenal to get what she wanted. So Bl</span>
  <span id="freeText7337700077405699607" style="display:none">Review posted at <a href="https://wp.me/p9u34A-5e" rel="nofollow noopener">The Chaise and Lounge Blog</a><br /><br />This audiobook was easy to follow and was a fun listen until I got the end. It was a happy ending but it reinforced that office romances can never remain secret and can make the workplace tense when there is a disharmony.<br /><br />Blair Walker was a girl who followed all of society rules of how a refined lady should behave. Living by that good girl code led her to losing her dreams to another who was willing to use all in her arsenal to get what she wanted. So Blair decided that she will throw out her list and just live without those constraints.<br />Life as a rebel led her to entrepreneur Richard Stratton, who was looking for someone to help him grow his online business. Their professional relationship thrived and was smooth until they developed an attraction. That's when things got awkward. Should they risk it or play it safe?<br /><br />I liked them together, but I am not a fan of office romances. They have a tendency to get messy when people have fights and/or break up. These sort of relationships are bad for business and it gets co-workers caught in the middle. There is workplace gossip as well as a resentment if there is a perception of favoritism.<br /><br />I really liked the new Blair until she threw a couple of unprofessional fits at end of the book because of her feelings for her boss Richard. I was embarrassed for her and for Richard. The new Blair was empowered, likable and interesting. Her journey showed development and maturity even though she was likable even with the list too. Both Blair and Richard were fundamentally good people with a great work ethic.<br /><br />Their relationship worked out in the end but I didn't like her doing the opposite of what her list would have told her to do. The list wasn't bad, I think she just needed to learn not to be so rigid. That is what life is about, having some flexibility in some things and being steadfast in others. Both Blair and Richard came to learn that in order to find true happiness, they had to be honest and true to themselves.<br /><br />If you want an enjoyable and easy read, then I recommend this office romance to satisfy that need.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7337700077405699607" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3014983009" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3014983009" />
    <a title="Bookworm" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31167656-bookworm"><img alt="Bookworm" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508209904p2/31167656.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3014983009?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookworm" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookworm" href="/user/show/31167656-bookworm">Bookworm</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3014983009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14159911697052074569">I realized that this book was not for me about a third of the way through. As a result, I ended up skimming most of it. Characters are one note and plot is way too predictable. Lacked the emotional depth I need in a contemporary romance. Reminded me of a B rated chick flick that works if you’re half asleep.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12124750610855252629">All of my reviews can be found on <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.novelgossip.com'>www.novelgossip.com</a><br/><br/>4.5/5<br/><br/>Last year I read the first book in this series, Love Connection and I adored it! While you can easily read I Have Never as a standalone, there are characters from the first book in this one as well. Plus, Isley has the unique ability to come up with a totally fresh premise for her books that is always so much fun, why would you wanna miss out?!<br/><br/>Blair is the ideal chick lit heroine, she's sweet, a little sassy and hilarious. When her perfec</span>
  <span id="freeText12124750610855252629" style="display:none">All of my reviews can be found on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.novelgossip.com">www.novelgossip.com</a><br /><br />4.5/5<br /><br />Last year I read the first book in this series, Love Connection and I adored it! While you can easily read I Have Never as a standalone, there are characters from the first book in this one as well. Plus, Isley has the unique ability to come up with a totally fresh premise for her books that is always so much fun, why would you wanna miss out?!<br /><br />Blair is the ideal chick lit heroine, she's sweet, a little sassy and hilarious. When her perfectly planned life starts to fall apart she decides to deviate from her list. What's on her list? Her rules for life, things like don't move in before you get a ring and don't get drunk. Instead of a bucket list it's basically the antithesis and the results were so funny! Richard from the first book is back, which totally made my day, I loved his character the first time around and catching up with him was a treat.<br /><br />One of my favorite things about reading an Isley book is that I find myself smiling the entire time. There is so much humor and warmth in her books and her lead characters are always super relatable and down to earth. Her writing style is as witty and charming as the characters she creates, if you're a fan of this genre and haven't read one of her books you're missing out! I hear book three in this series is a Christmas read which just makes me even more excited!</span>

The story is a great romcom style read. It's well written and engaging. Blaire is intelligent, strong and independent. The lesson here is to just live. Don't worry about rules because, whatever happens, the rules won'</span>
  <span id="freeText14588546750466453755" style="display:none">I Have Never is the story of Blaire. This is a woman who has always lived by a set of rules. But, even the rules can't stop her life from falling apart. When everything goes wrong, Blaire decides no more rules. She tries new and different things. The results are funny and charming. The story is a great romcom style read. It's well written and engaging. Blaire is intelligent, strong and independent. The lesson here is to just live. Don't worry about rules because, whatever happens, the rules won't save you from the pitfalls of life. Thanks to NetGalley for an arc in exchange for an honest review.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer677319317080409185">I'm reading the series backward, but it doesn't really matter as each story is self-contained and focuses on a different couple. <br/><br/>I loved this story so much, it had everything: A bucket list,but done in reverse (meaning Blair had a list of things not to do and suddenly decides to break bad and do them all), an office romance with a dishy boss, a cute puppy, a wonderful protagonist, and the best friends--and enemies. Also I love the game never have I ever and the way it was used as base narrative </span>
  <span id="freeText677319317080409185" style="display:none">I'm reading the series backward, but it doesn't really matter as each story is self-contained and focuses on a different couple. <br /><br />I loved this story so much, it had everything: A bucket list,but done in reverse (meaning Blair had a list of things not to do and suddenly decides to break bad and do them all), an office romance with a dishy boss, a cute puppy, a wonderful protagonist, and the best friends--and enemies. Also I love the game never have I ever and the way it was used as base narrative structure for this novel was so clever.<br /><br />Romantic, fun, hands-down one of my favorite chicklit books ever.</span>

  <span id="freeText15863044787514377407" style="display:none">I received a complimentary copy of this eBook from the author, publisher, and Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />When Blair Walker loses her boyfriend and job all in the same day, things don't turn out too well. It is only when her Never do list turns out to become her good luck charm giving her a new job and more. Is it all too good to be true or will she find love from it too? Read on and find out for yourself.<br /><br />This was a pretty good romantic comedy women's fiction book. I laughed, smiled and enjoyed reading about Blair's crazy escapades. If you enjoy funny romance books like this, I recommend you check this book out on Amazon and wherever books are sold. </span>

<div id="review_2714019130" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2714019130" />
    <a title="Kate R" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38708228-kate-r"><img alt="Kate R" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554674534p2/38708228.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2714019130?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kate R" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kate R" href="/user/show/38708228-kate-r">Kate R</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 1230001678987" href="/book/show/43845160-i-have-never">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38708228-kate-r?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2714019130" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11114866196742062946">This was a super quick, cute read that I really liked. I laughed out loud so many times in this book! This was my first read by the author and will not be my last. It is the second book in the First Comes Love series, but it’s a standalone. I haven’t read the first one and still enjoyed this one. <br/> <br/>I would probably qualify this more as a chick lit book. It’s not my usual genre and I haven’t read one in a few years, so I don’t remember if this is normal but, there was not a lot of descriptions or </span>
  <span id="freeText11114866196742062946" style="display:none">This was a super quick, cute read that I really liked. I laughed out loud so many times in this book! This was my first read by the author and will not be my last. It is the second book in the First Comes Love series, but it’s a standalone. I haven’t read the first one and still enjoyed this one. <br /> <br />I would probably qualify this more as a chick lit book. It’s not my usual genre and I haven’t read one in a few years, so I don’t remember if this is normal but, there was not a lot of descriptions or details about anything, unless it was talking about shoes or clothes (btw I would love to have her amazing wardrobe!). I really couldn’t tell you much about Blair, the main character. I loved Richard, the hero, but I had a lot of trouble with their lack of chemistry. <br /><br />I enjoyed many of the supporting characters: Indira, Christian, Nikki and of course, Chevron, the dog! The ending was so cute. I think Nikki and Christian are separately getting the next books in the series and I will definitely be reading those. I would recommend this especially if you're looking for a quick read and a good laugh!<br /><br />* ARC provided by NetGalley and the publisher in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11114866196742062946" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2068645418" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2068645418" />
    <a title="Carrie Schmidt (Reading is My SuperPower)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6084197-carrie-schmidt-reading-is-my-superpower"><img alt="Carrie Schmidt (Reading is My SuperPower)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576880537p2/6084197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2068645418?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carrie Schmidt (Reading is My SuperPower)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carrie Schmidt (Reading is My SuperPower)" href="/user/show/6084197-carrie-schmidt-reading-is-my-superpower">Carrie Schmidt (Reading is My SuperPower)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6084197-carrie-schmidt-reading-is-my-superpower?shelf=blog-reviewed">blog-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6084197-carrie-schmidt-reading-is-my-superpower?shelf=i-love-kissingbooks">i-love-kissingbooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6084197-carrie-schmidt-reading-is-my-superpower?shelf=romantic-fiction">romantic-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6084197-carrie-schmidt-reading-is-my-superpower?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2068645418" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2858966343765154201">Confession time: I totally grabbed this book because of the cover. I love the style, the colors, the whimsy. It makes me smile just looking at it. Yes, it seems that I’m suffering from an extreme case of cover love!<br/><br/>But the inside is just as delightful. I grinned through most of the story, except for those moments when I was holding my breath to see what Richard was going to do. Blair’s narrative voice is hilarious, snarky, and relatable. And let’s just talk about the romantical tension for a sec</span>
  <span id="freeText2858966343765154201" style="display:none">Confession time: I totally grabbed this book because of the cover. I love the style, the colors, the whimsy. It makes me smile just looking at it. Yes, it seems that I’m suffering from an extreme case of cover love!<br /><br />But the inside is just as delightful. I grinned through most of the story, except for those moments when I was holding my breath to see what Richard was going to do. Blair’s narrative voice is hilarious, snarky, and relatable. And let’s just talk about the romantical tension for a second. HOLY KISSINGBOOKS, BATMAN! Keep a fan handy for this read. The electricity between Richard and Blair could light up New York all on its own. I appreciated that Isley kept all the sexy times behind closed doors – just some kissing that will make you search for the nearest freezer and then fade to black. Blair sums it up for us later (which means you’ll be chuckling even as you fan yourself) but it’s still appropriate and classy. Isley does a fantastic job of conveying desire and emotion with a look… with a tight voice … with a text from an intrigued observer.<br /><br />Woven throughout these great characters and the off-the-charts chemistry is Blair’s reverse bucket list. Cleverly incorporated into the chapter titles, the items on Blair’s ‘never do’ list find her rather than vice versa. While she might think she’s setting out to check them off one-by-one, she rather stumbles into most of them, realizing many times after the fact that she could make this work for her list. It helped Blair – and the plot – seem even more engaging and likable.<br /><br />Bottom Line: I Have Never made me grin and fan and laugh out loud. I also cried, not gonna lie, because Isley is a master of charged emotions and tension. It’s a light chick lit read but it’s also sweet, sexy and lots of fun. You’ll fall in love with Blair, Chevron, and of course Richard and his brooding British-accented self. It’s rare for me to find a romcom that I go back and re-read right away, but I did go back and find some of my favorite snippets to swoon over again. <br /><br />(I voluntarily reviewed a complimentary copy of this book)<br /><br />**Readers may want to be aware that there is cursing in this novel**<br /><br />see my review at <a href="http://readingismysuperpower.org/2017/07/18/book-review-giveaway-never-camilla-isley/" rel="nofollow noopener">Reading Is My SuperPower</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2858966343765154201" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2688910826?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danny" href="/user/show/37372292-danny">Danny</a>
      </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3760078962506746455">Ok... The first thing I need to say and the thing that caught my eye the most was that this was not a story that circled only on the romance and "insta-love" thing. I really liked that Blair was really focused on her career and loved what she did.<br/>The first chapters are full of her getting back on her feet and snatching successful jobs and ideas for the new magazine. This was really awesome. She was determined and focused on creating a magazine department from the ground up.<br/>The romance was built </span>
  <span id="freeText3760078962506746455" style="display:none">Ok... The first thing I need to say and the thing that caught my eye the most was that this was not a story that circled only on the romance and "insta-love" thing. I really liked that Blair was really focused on her career and loved what she did.<br />The first chapters are full of her getting back on her feet and snatching successful jobs and ideas for the new magazine. This was really awesome. She was determined and focused on creating a magazine department from the ground up.<br />The romance was built right along with her career, and that was so good to read. One of the best aspects of this book, for me.<br /><br />Anyway... I love Camilla's books. Her writing is great and I find myself always laughing with her stories.<br />This one was no different.<br /><br />Blair had everything planned for her life but one day everything went crumbling down. <br />That's when she snaps and see that her plan for life, based on being always the nice person and always remain calm, she see that it was all for nothing.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>It’s all been for nothing. All the sacrifices I made. All the times I said, “No,” to anything even remotely fun. All the lost opportunities… to live rather than just behave.<br />(...)<br />Not being in control is great. Not holding back is fantastic. I should’ve done it a long time ago. I should’ve done so many things. All my life, I’ve had it backward. I’ve spent years caged behind the bars of the list, never allowing myself a moment of fun. That’s over. The list’s regime ends now.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />And that's when she really starts living.<br />Her new job at a new magazine brings her everything she didn't know was missing. The great atmosphere, great friends, and the most important having fun doing something she loves.<br />Indira was the best! I loved her and laughed so much with her antics!<br /><br />I just loved this romantic comedy. It's warm and light, it left me with a warm feeling inside and I kind of wish to experience some of those situations some day.</span>

  <span id="freeText8565104777165055916" style="display:none">Blair has an amazing job and an amazing boyfriend. One day is all it takes to lose both. She finds herself following a list of things to never do and when she decides to change her life, she begins to go against everything on that list. She soon gets a new job and she begins to fall for her boss, Richard, a man completely against relationships and commitment. This is not a good thing for Blair, but maybe life can change for the better. <br /><br />I loved this book. It was such a fun, dramatic, and yes, a little steamy romance. I loved Blair. She has her life all planned out and when that comes crashing down, she goes against all she knows and takes life on with bravery. She is an awesome character. I absolutely love the romance of this book. It was so real and hard. Love is never easy.<br /><br />Overall this book was written well and had me so enthralled I read it in one sitting. <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.boundlessbookreviews.com">http://www.boundlessbookreviews.com</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/BBReviews">https://www.facebook.com/BBReviews</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2007420715?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leah" href="/user/show/2641242-leah">Leah</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2641242-leah?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2641242-leah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2641242-leah?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2641242-leah?shelf=books-read-2017">books-read-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2007420715" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2424847831311441233"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499682649i/23257133._SX540_.png' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Camilla Isley has quickly become one of my favourite Chick Lit writers. Her style, her plots, her fabulous characters, they all add up to pretty fantastic reads - and quick ones, too! I didn't plan to devour I Have Never in pretty much one sitting, but I did and I don't regret it. I loved Blair, and Richard, and Chevron the dog (oh, did I love Chevron the dog!) and I loved that after her firing (redundancy?) and her break-up, Blair decided to tear up her old list, of ways a lady should act at al</span>
  <span id="freeText2424847831311441233" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499682649i/23257133._SX540_.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Camilla Isley has quickly become one of my favourite Chick Lit writers. Her style, her plots, her fabulous characters, they all add up to pretty fantastic reads - and quick ones, too! I didn't plan to devour I Have Never in pretty much one sitting, but I did and I don't regret it. I loved Blair, and Richard, and Chevron the dog (oh, did I love Chevron the dog!) and I loved that after her firing (redundancy?) and her break-up, Blair decided to tear up her old list, of ways a lady should act at all times (not making a scene, don't go skinny dipping, don't get arrested) and do the exact opposites of all those don'ts on her list. And it's <em>brilliant</em>.<br><br>Blair was such a brilliant character - I loved her from the word go, and it's pretty hard NOT to like somebody who throws a plate of spaghetti onto someone else's head. That immediately gets hero status from me. That's the kind of stuff I dream of being brave enough to do, but I could never do, because it would be so out of character for me, so I love to live vicariously through my MCs in books. To then tear up her list of rules for being proper and ladylike, made the book even better (obviously), leading to many hilarious scenes including (but not limited to): acquiring a dog at a petrol station, getting arrested and spending a few hours in jail, and waking up in a strange man's bed and finding out he's the hottest man, ever. It was thoroughly entertaining.<br><br>The banter between Richard and Blair was pretty off the charts. It was frustrating, because you could tell Richard was holding back, but it was also exciting. I love when a romance makes me excited, when I'm ready for them to kiss, and even that ridiculous Aurora subplot didn't dampen my excitement (especially because Blair got to explode like a firecracker). I just loved everything about I Have Never, *especially* the game of Never Have I Ever near to the end. I got all those swooshy feelings and UGH it was incredible. I'm such a sucker for these types of books, and I loved rooting for Blair on every page. It was just a brilliant, brilliant read and I can't wait to read more from Camilla Isley, she's a cracking writer.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498300378i/23113713._SX540_.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2424847831311441233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2051571660" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2051571660" />
    <a title="Kaisha (The Writing Garnet)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40776578-kaisha-the-writing-garnet"><img alt="Kaisha (The Writing Garnet)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425216397p2/40776578.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2051571660?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kaisha (The Writing Garnet)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kaisha (The Writing Garnet)" href="/user/show/40776578-kaisha-the-writing-garnet">Kaisha (The Writing Garnet)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2051571660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17524890564516090984">All reviews can be found on my blog at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://thewritinggarnet.wordpress.com'>https://thewritinggarnet.wordpress.com</a><br/><br/>I am a HUGE, HUGE fan of Camilla Isley's novels so as soon as I found out that I could read her newest one, AND be part of her blog tour, I felt like all my birthdays had come at once! Just like Ms.Isley's other novels, 'I Have Never' is another novel which has you thinking 'this sounds familiar!' by the end of the first chapter (also known as - super relatable). <br/><br/>Blair has always been the type of girl to stick to a list</span>
  <span id="freeText17524890564516090984" style="display:none">All reviews can be found on my blog at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://thewritinggarnet.wordpress.com">https://thewritinggarnet.wordpress.com</a><br /><br />I am a HUGE, HUGE fan of Camilla Isley's novels so as soon as I found out that I could read her newest one, AND be part of her blog tour, I felt like all my birthdays had come at once! Just like Ms.Isley's other novels, 'I Have Never' is another novel which has you thinking 'this sounds familiar!' by the end of the first chapter (also known as - super relatable). <br /><br />Blair has always been the type of girl to stick to a list; her five-year plan if you will. As far as she's concerned the list is there to be abided by, not to go against. However, poor Blair seems to have picked the short straw as luck doesn't seem to be on her side, especially as in one day she lost her job AND her boyfriend. Eeesh!<br /><br />Blair has the type of personality a lot of women would admire, I know I certainly did! She's sassy, feisty, knows her own mind yet has a heart of gold. The only thing that she struggles with is letting go. Until now.<br /><br />Even though 'I Have Never' is the second book in the First Comes Love series, it can be read as a standalone. That said, the first book in the series is brilliant as well! May as well buy both then eh!<br /><br />In all honesty, I don't think I read this book without a smile on my face. The entire storyline was written brilliantly, it's such a fun and uplifting novel, which, in my opinion, isn't the vibe you get from the book to begin with. As always, Camilla Isley's trademark humour oozes from the storyline AND the characters. I think I spent most of the time giggling at Richard's antics or the puppy's legendary communication skills.<br /><br />For me, the best part of 'I Have Never' was the backwards bucket list - absolutely fantastic idea. Because of that, I was able to see Blair come out of her shell in a different way, it was as though she had learnt to find comfort within herself. Lovely to read.<br /><br />I am having withdrawal symptoms already, I cannot WAIT for another Camilla Isley novel to be released. Such pocket-sized perfection, every single time. I LOVED this book, you will definitely be a numpty not to read this.<br /><br />Thanks Camilla &amp; Aimee B.</span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<div id="review_2028574864" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2028574864" />
    <a title="Ishita" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44403487-ishita"><img alt="Ishita" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1449085817p2/44403487.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2028574864?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ishita" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ishita" href="/user/show/44403487-ishita">Ishita</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2028574864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16974846381902866641">How would you react after going through the worst day of your life? Well, the most sorted thing to do is probably make a “sensible” To-Do list and re-evaluate. But, for Blair, who has always carried and meticulously lived by an actual list of Do’s and Don’ts on paper, this is an opportunity to put the list through a figurative shredder.<br/><br/>I loved the premise as soon as I read the synopsis because I thought it was a pretty cool idea to use the oft-employed idea of “bucket-list” but with a twist. It </span>
  <span id="freeText16974846381902866641" style="display:none">How would you react after going through the worst day of your life? Well, the most sorted thing to do is probably make a “sensible” To-Do list and re-evaluate. But, for Blair, who has always carried and meticulously lived by an actual list of Do’s and Don’ts on paper, this is an opportunity to put the list through a figurative shredder.<br /><br />I loved the premise as soon as I read the synopsis because I thought it was a pretty cool idea to use the oft-employed idea of “bucket-list” but with a twist. It works pretty well, each chapter is named after something from the list, so it sets the stage nicely for events to come. It is fun trying to guess how exactly would Blair end up doing(or not!) everything she never planned on before her life upended.<br /><br />After getting fired and nursing a broken heart, she lands a job at an online-editorial portal. Here, she makes new friends, gets a chance to build an entire fashion/beauty magazine from scratch and finds it more fulfilling than her previous high-profile job. There is another major factor contributing to her happiness too – her boss whom she has been majorly crushing on right from their first accidental encounter. The boss here is Richard, who featured in the first book of this series. Richard, who got ditched at the altar in the previous book, is understandably commitment-phobic and well , just a bit averse to having any girlfriend lasting more than a month. The book centers largely on Blair figuring out whether Richard is interested in taking their relationship beyond the professional realm and Richard getting over his fears after the incidents in the previous book.<br /><br />This book can be read as a standalone so, if you are wondering about whether to pick this up before the first one, I would say that it wouldn’t be a problem. But, I personally enjoyed the references to the previous book. My favorite (and the most direct one) was Blair confiding her feelings for Richard to an airport bartender who featured in the previous book. Most of the other references were lingering ones related to Richard’s ex. Considering that most chicklits are from the girl’s PoV, I feel that the male MC’s character arc is usually rushed or underdeveloped. But Richard’s was actually done pretty well. I liked how the author showed him being “ready” to take the relationship forward but probably at a different pace than what he thought Blair expected of him. It actually made all the “conflicts” between them at the end of the book feel realistic rather than something that was hurriedly thrust into the last pages just to amp up the drama.<br /><br />With LA celebrities, snarky interviews at fashion houses, takedowns featuring spaghetti-dunking and fake lawsuits, and an adorable puppy, this was very entertaining and a great addition to the series! And just to add to the list of things I loved – Blair’s love for heels, the whole start-up team working for Richard (and yay, it actually mentions the techies too! No seriously, the techies are never mentioned in any of the “magazine/fashion” business set-ups in books. As if the online portals magically run by themselves….), and the clever way in which Blair ends up negating the “eating meat” caveat of her list (as she is a vegetarian). Respect!<br /><br />*<i><b>Note</b> : I received an e-arc of this book from the author in exchange for an honest review. Review first posted on bookmyopia/wordpress*</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16974846381902866641" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2067288140" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2067288140" />
    <a title="Alison" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27476718-alison"><img alt="Alison" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451665348p2/27476718.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2067288140?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alison" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alison" href="/user/show/27476718-alison">Alison</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/35155266-i-have-never">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2067288140" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5053946816313201322">I’m a fan of Camilla Isley so I was fairly confident I would be in for a treat with I Have Never and oh boy was I right. I think I giggled out loud quite a few times in this book all at poor Blair’s expense.<br/><br/>Blair Walker thinks life is all mapped out and perfect, late twenties, great job, perfect boyfriend then wham .. the job and the boyfriend are gone so what can she do next!?<br/><br/>She has always lived by rules and has a list of things not to do in order to have a good life .. so what will happen if </span>
  <span id="freeText5053946816313201322" style="display:none">I’m a fan of Camilla Isley so I was fairly confident I would be in for a treat with I Have Never and oh boy was I right. I think I giggled out loud quite a few times in this book all at poor Blair’s expense.<br /><br />Blair Walker thinks life is all mapped out and perfect, late twenties, great job, perfect boyfriend then wham .. the job and the boyfriend are gone so what can she do next!?<br /><br />She has always lived by rules and has a list of things not to do in order to have a good life .. so what will happen if this list is reversed! <br /><br />Such things on her list as: Never Lie, Never Mix Business and Pleasure, Never Make a Scene, Don’t move in without a ring and many others all get turned on their head with either hilarious or disastrous consequences.<br /><br />Each chapter has a ‘list’ heading, so easy to read, wickedly engaging, this captured my interest from beginning to end. I can’t think of anything in this book not to love and enjoy. Not overly long so it’s simple to read in one glorious sitting.<br /><br />A deliciously handsome man, a cute as a button dog and Blair who I adored .. what more could I ask for!? Superb entertainment.<br /><br />My thanks to Camilla and Aimee for my copy which I read and reviewed voluntarily.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2077019643" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2077019643" />
    <a title="Marivi Sanz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12555693-marivi-sanz"><img alt="Marivi Sanz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346876121p2/12555693.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2077019643?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marivi Sanz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marivi Sanz" href="/user/show/12555693-marivi-sanz">Marivi Sanz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12555693-marivi-sanz?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12555693-marivi-sanz?shelf=romantic-comedy">romantic-comedy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12555693-marivi-sanz?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12555693-marivi-sanz?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2077019643" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12042396334760878397">After reading (and enjoying) "Love connection", I decided to read the second book in the series, "I have never". Though it can be read as a stand alone book, it follows the story of a character from the first book, Richard, the guy left at the altar by the protagonist.<br/><br/>Blake Walker wakes up one day excited about the brilliant prospects before her: she's going to get promoted at work, and her boyfriend is going to propose that night. But somehow, that perfect day turns into the perfect nightmare, </span>
  <span id="freeText12042396334760878397" style="display:none">After reading (and enjoying) "Love connection", I decided to read the second book in the series, "I have never". Though it can be read as a stand alone book, it follows the story of a character from the first book, Richard, the guy left at the altar by the protagonist.<br /><br />Blake Walker wakes up one day excited about the brilliant prospects before her: she's going to get promoted at work, and her boyfriend is going to propose that night. But somehow, that perfect day turns into the perfect nightmare, when she's not only not promoted, but fired, and her boyfriend dumps her after admitting he'd been cheating on her.<br /><br />After having lived all her life following the rules, she decides to take that list of rules and do exactly the opposite to see where that leads her.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this book. The premise was not the usual "bucket-list" story, the characters are really well developed, and the writing style is easy to read (I read it in one sitting).<br /><br />Definitely, I'll read more of her books. They are perfect for a lazy day at home.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12042396334760878397" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2089581622" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2089581622" />
    <a title="Paula Figueira" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69234403-paula-figueira"><img alt="Paula Figueira" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1502195528p2/69234403.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2089581622?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula Figueira" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula Figueira" href="/user/show/69234403-paula-figueira">Paula Figueira</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/35155266-i-have-never">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2089581622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11310739897316011599">I can't even express my love for this book right now! I read it in only a few hours, because it is so catchy that I couldn't stop reading it, it fascinated me in every way.<br/>I think the writing of the writer and the division of the chapters are magnificent.<br/>The way of living life presented in this book is very different from what we are accustomed to, but it is the right way and it is how we should all look at life because we often let ourselves be limited by our fears and we are not truly happy.<br/>Th</span>
  <span id="freeText11310739897316011599" style="display:none">I can't even express my love for this book right now! I read it in only a few hours, because it is so catchy that I couldn't stop reading it, it fascinated me in every way.<br />I think the writing of the writer and the division of the chapters are magnificent.<br />The way of living life presented in this book is very different from what we are accustomed to, but it is the right way and it is how we should all look at life because we often let ourselves be limited by our fears and we are not truly happy.<br />The characters are passionate and entertaining and the whole story seems very realistic, which almost makes it seem like we are living within the story and not just reading it. I highly value the way the romance between Blair and Richard has evolved, valuing feelings rather than just sex, as it happens in several books, which also helps us to fall more in love with the story of this couple.<br />I give it 5 stars and could not be happier with my reading, I recommend it without a doubt and I can't wait to read the other books of Camilla Isley !</span>
  <a data-text-id="11310739897316011599" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18090304060766294914">Chuckle-out-loud RomCom. (Real men do not giggle.)<br/><br/>What it says on the cover. Nicely constructed quick-paced comedy romance with an adult tone and wonderful wit. Richard is a Hunk (I'm a man and even I can tell how tasty he is!) Blair is a height-sensitive New York redhead with recent wounds that make her understandably hair-triggered. Her decision to throw out her rulebook for life begins with getting drunk and staggers on with increasing chuckles from there. This was great fun and very satisfyi</span>
  <span id="freeText18090304060766294914" style="display:none">Chuckle-out-loud RomCom. (Real men do not giggle.)<br /><br />What it says on the cover. Nicely constructed quick-paced comedy romance with an adult tone and wonderful wit. Richard is a Hunk (I'm a man and even I can tell how tasty he is!) Blair is a height-sensitive New York redhead with recent wounds that make her understandably hair-triggered. Her decision to throw out her rulebook for life begins with getting drunk and staggers on with increasing chuckles from there. This was great fun and very satisfying. Chevron, however, was my favourite character in the book.<br /><br />P.S. This is a completely independent story, fine to read on its own.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2708886093" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16659069866381329899">5 stars<br/>This is my first book from Camilla Isley, and it wont be the last.<br/>I loved this book! <br/>Blair lives her life through a series of "rules", but when her boyfriend of three years breaks up with her the same week she loses her job Blair loses her temper and decides no more rules! <br/>I love the concept of this book, it's so funny and lovable. I loved the work dynamic between the characters and their banter. <br/>Thank you to netgalley for providing this article in return of an honest review.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2795209407" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2795209407" />
    <a title="Rachel McMillan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2201736-rachel-mcmillan"><img alt="Rachel McMillan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1453601105p2/2201736.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2795209407?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel McMillan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel McMillan" href="/user/show/2201736-rachel-mcmillan">Rachel McMillan</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2795209407" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11894660853229127474">This is a case of the voice, setting and heroine working really well for me but the trope not being a favourite.<br/><br/>Just a personal preference and no reflection on the author or story, but the woman falling for boss thing and pursuing a romantic relationship that intersects with personal ambition just isn't totally my thing. <br/><br/><br/>I felt that the story had a bit of a Shopaholic thing going on: what with the boss being enamoured with a competitor of the heroine from a previous job.<br/><br/><br/>Alongside a gorgeously se</span>
  <span id="freeText11894660853229127474" style="display:none">This is a case of the voice, setting and heroine working really well for me but the trope not being a favourite.<br /><br />Just a personal preference and no reflection on the author or story, but the woman falling for boss thing and pursuing a romantic relationship that intersects with personal ambition just isn't totally my thing. <br /><br /><br />I felt that the story had a bit of a Shopaholic thing going on: what with the boss being enamoured with a competitor of the heroine from a previous job.<br /><br /><br />Alongside a gorgeously set Manhattan and jaunt to L.A., Blair's lists of "nevers" was a fresh and winning way to structure an immensely readable novel.<br /><br />I will definitely be reading more by this author: she has a bright sense of humour and a keen handle on character.<br /><br /><br />With thanks to Netgalley.</span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zHoKSGZFXXv+qbssMwLIwZyjwROH5Mgs73l5/E7EzQb2XGOa3RuUE1mCD03E98IeSvwm20lpRku0Bz9Ng4c/nA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Q9ILb7rHKdcV5rGxhDzb5m5d/IG1EfMH46Mkli6Sk1159GK9AZngv7LNBdBzydE5uAIbSXucfWC43WIn49Fhxw==')})
  }
